[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability has been detected during fuzzing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the Apache POI library. The vulnerability was triggered when processing XSSF [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mExcel[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m files, specifically during the extraction of extended properties. The [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer detected an attempted connection to `jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m`, indicating that [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted data from the input file was used to make an external network request [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout proper validation.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis issue represents a Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability classified[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas a medium severity security issue. The vulnerability occurs when the Apache POI [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary processes Excel files [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXSSF format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and attempts to make network [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnections based on data contained within the file without adequate validation or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitization.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mServer Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m allows an attacker to cause the server-side [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplication to make HTTP requests to arbitrary domains. This can lead to:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exfiltration of sensitive data[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exposure of internal services[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Potential access to resources that should not be accessible from external sources[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Scanning of internal network infrastructure[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Trigger Point**: The vulnerability is triggered during XML parsing when [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing extended properties of an XSSF file. The stack trace shows the issue [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginates from `[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Network Activity**: The system attempted to establish a socket connection to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m`, indicating that the hostname was extracted from the fuzzer input [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand used to initiate an HTTP connection.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Call Chain**: The vulnerability manifests through the following execution [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - XML parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mSAXParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Entity reference scanning [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mXMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl.scanEntityReference[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Entity manager setup [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.setupCurrentEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.startEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - HTTP connection establishment [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mHttpURLConnection.connect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Socket connection [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mSocket.connect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **XML External Entity Processing**: The stack trace indicates that the XML [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser is attempting to resolve external entity references, which is a common [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvector for SSRF attacks. The parser is following external references defined in the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML content without proper restrictions.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas Requiring Investigation[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo obtain a comprehensive understanding of this vulnerability, the following [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents should be examined:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor Class** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m316[0m[39m in `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLine [0m[1;36m299[0m[39m in `[0m[1;35mgetText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How extended properties are extracted from XSSF files[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - XML parsing configuration and entity resolution handling[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether external entity processing is enabled[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **XML Parser Configuration**:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - SAXParser initialization and configuration settings[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Feature flags related to external entity processing[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Document Type Definition [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDTD[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m processing settings[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - XML External Entity [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXXE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m prevention measures[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **XMLEntityManager**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How external entities are resolved[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - URL validation and sanitization mechanisms [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether there are allowlists or blocklists for entity resolution[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **POI Package Structure**:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `org.apache.poi.xssf.extractor` package and related XML processing utilities[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Common XML parsing patterns used across the codebase[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Security configurations for XML processors[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Input Validation**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether there are any mechanisms to validate or sanitize URLs before [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnection attempts[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Restrictions on protocols and domains that can be accessed[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Network access controls within the POI library[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability appears to be a classic XML External Entity [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXXE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m injection issue[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat leads to SSRF, where maliciously crafted XLSX files can contain references to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal resources that the parser will attempt to fetch.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy for SSRF Vulnerability in XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability exists in [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`poi-ooxml/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/xssf/extractor/XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m.java` at line [0m[1;36m315[0m[39m in the `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method. The code creates an insecure[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParser using `[0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` without any [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity configuration, allowing XML External Entity [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXXE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m resolution that leads to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mServer Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Vulnerable Code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m315[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis creates a parser with default settings that:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Allow DOCTYPE declarations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXXE attack vector[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Allow external entity resolution [0m[1;39m([0m[39mleads to SSRF when malicious XLSX files contain[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity references to external URLs[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Don't restrict entity expansion[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Implementation[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Primary Fix: Replace insecure SAXParser creation with secure XMLHelper utility**[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase already provides `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which creates a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperly secured SAXParserFactory. The fix requires replacing the insecure parser [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstantiation with the secure alternative.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Specific Changes to `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.java`:**[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace lines [0m[1;36m314[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m316[0m[39m:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtry [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mpart.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, new [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtry [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mpart.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, new [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key Change:** Replace `[0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Why This Fix is Optimal[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Minimal Code Change:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only one line needs modification [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m315[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The existing `ExtendedPropertiesHandler` class [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m485[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m543[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The parsing logic and exception handling remain identical[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Import statement for `XMLHelper` already exists at line [0m[1;36m48[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Uses Established Secure Pattern:**[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` configures the parser with:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING = true`[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `FEATURE_LOAD_DTD_GRAMMAR = false`[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `FEATURE_LOAD_EXTERNAL_DTD = false`[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `FEATURE_EXTERNAL_ENTITIES = false` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprevents XXE/SSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `FEATURE_DISALLOW_DOCTYPE_DECL = true` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mblocks DOCTYPE-based attacks[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Consistent with Codebase Patterns:**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The same class already uses `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in `[0m[1;35mprocessSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m251[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Test file `ExcelFileFormatDocFunctionExtractor.java` demonstrates the pattern at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m435[0m[39m: `SAXParserFactory sf = [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Multiple parts of the codebase use XMLHelper for secure XML parsing[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Preserves Existing Functionality:**[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The SAXParser API remains identical[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `ExtendedPropertiesHandler` receives the same SAX events[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Test expectations [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mtestExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at lines [0m[1;36m307[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m313[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to pass[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Output format [0m[32m"Extended Properties:\n[0m[32m{[0m[32mPropertyName[0m[32m}[0m[32m: [0m[32m{[0m[32mvalue[0m[32m}[0m[32m\n..."[0m[39m remains [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Special handling for AppVersion and MajorVersion extraction is preserved[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Security Guarantees[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix provides comprehensive protection against:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m XML External Entity [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXXE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Attacks:**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `FEATURE_EXTERNAL_ENTITIES = false` prevents resolution of external general [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentities[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `FEATURE_DISALLOW_DOCTYPE_DECL = true` blocks DOCTYPE declarations that enable [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXXE[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- External entity resolution is disabled, preventing the parser from making HTTP [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnections to attacker-controlled domains[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The specific issue [0m[32m"Attempted connection to: jazze.com:80"[0m[39m will be prevented[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Entity Expansion Attacks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBillion Laughs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `FEATURE_LOAD_DTD_GRAMMAR = false` and `FEATURE_LOAD_EXTERNAL_DTD = false` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevent DTD-based expansion attacks[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Impact on Inherited Classes[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix automatically protects `XSSFBEventBasedExcelExtractor` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich extends [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor` at line [0m[1;36m47[0m[39m of `XSSFBEventBasedExcelExtractor.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msince it inherits the `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method without overriding it.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. No Breaking Changes[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Test Compatibility:**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing tests continue to work, including `[0m[1;35mtestExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidates the extraction of [0m[32m"AppVersion: 14.0300"[0m[39m and [0m[32m"MajorVersion: 14"[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `[0m[1;35msnipProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` helper method remains valid[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m API Compatibility:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Public methods and their signatures remain unchanged[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exception handling remains the same [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcatches ParserConfigurationException, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXException, IOException[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The method is private, so external callers are not affected[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Functionality Preservation:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Extended properties are still extracted from XLSX files[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The output format remains identical[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Performance characteristics are similar [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSAXParser from secure factory has [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnegligible overhead[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Alternative Approaches Considered and Rejected[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Use [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with XMLReader API**[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXMLReader xmlReader = [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mxmlReader.setContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mxmlReader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected because:** Requires more code changes [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m lines vs [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m line[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and changes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe parsing API from SAXParser to XMLReader, though both approaches are equally [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecure.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Use XMLBeans [0m[1;35mFactory.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m like POIXMLProperties**[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPropertiesDocument props = [0m[1;35mPropertiesDocument.Factory.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEFAULT_XML_[0m[1;33mOPTIONS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Extract properties from props object[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected because:** Requires rewriting the entire extraction logic, replacing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAX event handling with XMLBeans object model traversal. This is a much larger [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchange that's harder to test and validate.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Manual security configuration**[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParserFactory factory = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mfactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://apache.org/xml/features/disallow-doctype-decl"[0m[39m, true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mfactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://xml.org/sax/features/external-general-entities"[0m[39m, false[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m more feature settings[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mfactory.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected because:** Duplicates security configuration logic already centralized[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min XMLHelper, violating DRY principle and making it harder to maintain security [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstandards consistently across the codebase.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m. Verification Strategy[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying the fix, verify:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Security:**[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer should no longer detect SSRF attempts[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- External entity references in XLSX files should be ignored[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No network connections should be attempted during extended property extraction[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Functionality:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Run `[0m[1;35mtestExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` test to confirm extended properties are still extracted[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Verify output format matches expected [0m[32m"Extended Properties:\n[0m[32m{[0m[32mPropertyName[0m[32m}[0m[32m: [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m{[0m[32mvalue[0m[32m}[0m[32m\n..."[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Confirm AppVersion and MajorVersion extraction still works[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Compatibility:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing unit tests in `TestXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor` should pass[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Integration tests using the extractor should continue to function[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m. Summary[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy addresses the SSRF vulnerability by replacing one line of [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsecure code with a secure alternative already provided by the codebase. It [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleverages existing security utilities, maintains full backward compatibility, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserves all functionality, and aligns with established patterns used throughout [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApache POI. The fix is minimal, safe, and effective.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
